12.8 2014.10.08 1.  Command Table 수정 
 - 지원함으로 변경 : 0x4b, 0x75, 0x9c, 0x9d SQE   
 - 지원안함으로 변경 : 0x01, 0x03, 0x4f, 0x74, 0x81, 0x88, 0x8c, 0x8d, 
0x8e, 0x90, 0x91, 0x93 
 - 0xc8, OnScreen Display control command 추가 
  
2. 0x8b, Video Wall Direct User Control 
 - Table 값 15x15 기준으로 수정 
 - Input source table 을 삭제하고 0x14 input command 의 table 을 
참조하도록 명기함 
 - Wall_Div table 을 삭제하고 0x89, Video Wall User Control command 의 
table 을 참조하도록 명기함 
 - Wall_Sno table 을 삭제하고 0x89, Video Wall User Control 
command 의 table 을 참조하도록 명기함 
  
3. 0x3f, Color Temperature Control 
 - table hex value 추가 
  
4. 0x63, Ticker 
 - ticker msg max 25 자로 수정(Menu 동일사양) 
5. 0xc8, OnScreen Display control command 추가 
12.9 2014.11.19 
1.  Command Table 수정 
  - 지원함/지원하지 않음 내용 삭제(별도 table 관리) 
  - Data Type 세부 정리 
2. Smart Signage 에서 사용하지 않는 Command 삭제 
    : 제품팀 검토결과 사용하지 않는 Cmd – 0x0a, 0x1f, 0x20, 0x21, 
0x22, 0x23, 0x35, 0x39, 0x3a, 0x3b, 0x46, 0x49 0x82, 0x98, 0x99, 0x9a, 
0x9b 
    : 정체불명(table 에는 있으나 세부 command 설명 없음) – 0x0c, 0x1a, 
0x1b 0x1c, 0x5e, 0x60, 0x7B, 0x7c, 0x7d, 0xdd,  
  
2. 0x14, Input Source Control (MFM) 
  - WiDi -> WiDi/Screen Mirroring 
  
3. 0x85, Temperature Control 
  - Input range is changed as 75~124 
  
4. 0x5B, Screen Burn Timer 
  - T.Time 값 10~50 sec 으로 수정 및 code table 추가 
  
5. 0x87, Dynamic Contrast 
  - Limitation 변경 → 모든 Source 에서 동작하며 특정 Picture 
Mode 에서만 동작함 
6. 0x18, Screen Mode Control  
  - Limitation 변경 → It will work on Video Wall Off, Landscape or 
Picture size is Auto Wide. (Picture Size Auto Wide is only used on 
European Tuner Signal) 
SQE   
13.0 2014.12.18 
1. 0x14, Input Source Control 
   - 설명추가 : 0x60 → Media/MagicInfo S 
   - Source 추가 : 0x64 – IWB(Get only), 0x55 – HDBaseT 
  
2. 문서 전 영역에서 AM : 1 / PM : 0 으로 표기하여 혼선을 없앰 
  
3. 0xc8, OnScreen Display control 
   - Orientation option 변경 : Landscape(0), Portrait(270), 180, 90 
   - 0x84, NetPIP Rotation subcommand 추가 
  
4. 0x15, Picture Size Control 
   - 신규 mode – 21:9 및 note 추가 
 
5. 0x10, Model Number Control 
- NT 계열 모델 정리    
- GolfS 계열 모델 추가 
    - QMD105 모델 추가 
 
6. 0x83, Panel On time 
   - 설명추가 : 10 분당 1 count 증가 
SQE   
 
7. 0x20, Model Number Control 
   - Panel type 추가 
13.1 2015.02.03 
1. 0xc8, Onscreen Display control 
- 0x84, PIP Rotation : 제약사항 Note 추가 
 
2. 0x10, Model Number Control 
- 모델 추가 0x55 : RH48E, RH55E 
- 모델 추가 0x4f : OH46D, OH55D 
 
3. 0xb6, DST Control 
- DST 설정시 Month range 수정 : 00 ~ 0C -> 00 ~ 0b 
 
4. 0xb7, Custom PIP Control 
- 설정범위 오류 수정 :  
  Note : The PIP Start Position and Size do not over panel H, V size 
  H/V Size : 512 * 288 ~ 1632 * 918  ( Interval : 160 pixel ) 
  512*288, 672*378, 832*468, 992*558, 1152*648, 1312*738,  
1472*828, 1632*918 
 
5. 0x2e, Balance Control 
- GolfS 에서 변경된 사양 Note 로 추가 
 
6. 신규 cmd 추가 
- 0x1a, Outdoor mode control 
- 0x8c, Video Wall Feature control 
- 0xba, Upgrade Control 
 
7. 0xc4, Supported Function Control 
- Add a new format for adding FWUpdate protocol status 
SPD

12.8 2014.10.08 1.  Command Table 수정 
 - 지원함으로 변경 : 0x4b, 0x75, 0x9c, 0x9d SQE   
 - 지원안함으로 변경 : 0x01, 0x03, 0x4f, 0x74, 0x81, 0x88, 0x8c, 0x8d, 
0x8e, 0x90, 0x91, 0x93 
 - 0xc8, OnScreen Display control command 추가 
  
2. 0x8b, Video Wall Direct User Control 
 - Table 값 15x15 기준으로 수정 
 - Input source table 을 삭제하고 0x14 input command 의 table 을 
참조하도록 명기함 
 - Wall_Div table 을 삭제하고 0x89, Video Wall User Control command 의 
table 을 참조하도록 명기함 
 - Wall_Sno table 을 삭제하고 0x89, Video Wall User Control 
command 의 table 을 참조하도록 명기함 
  
3. 0x3f, Color Temperature Control 
 - table hex value 추가 
  
4. 0x63, Ticker 
 - ticker msg max 25 자로 수정(Menu 동일사양) 
5. 0xc8, OnScreen Display control command 추가 
12.9 2014.11.19 
1.  Command Table 수정 
  - 지원함/지원하지 않음 내용 삭제(별도 table 관리) 
  - Data Type 세부 정리 
2. Smart Signage 에서 사용하지 않는 Command 삭제 
    : 제품팀 검토결과 사용하지 않는 Cmd – 0x0a, 0x1f, 0x20, 0x21, 
0x22, 0x23, 0x35, 0x39, 0x3a, 0x3b, 0x46, 0x49 0x82, 0x98, 0x99, 0x9a, 
0x9b 
    : 정체불명(table 에는 있으나 세부 command 설명 없음) – 0x0c, 0x1a, 
0x1b 0x1c, 0x5e, 0x60, 0x7B, 0x7c, 0x7d, 0xdd,  
  
2. 0x14, Input Source Control (MFM) 
  - WiDi -> WiDi/Screen Mirroring 
  
3. 0x85, Temperature Control 
  - Input range is changed as 75~124 
  
4. 0x5B, Screen Burn Timer 
  - T.Time 값 10~50 sec 으로 수정 및 code table 추가 
  
5. 0x87, Dynamic Contrast 
  - Limitation 변경 → 모든 Source 에서 동작하며 특정 Picture 
Mode 에서만 동작함 
6. 0x18, Screen Mode Control  
  - Limitation 변경 → It will work on Video Wall Off, Landscape or 
Picture size is Auto Wide. (Picture Size Auto Wide is only used on 
European Tuner Signal) 
SQE

1. Interface 
 
1.1. Connection Method  
There are 2 available ways of connecting. One is RS232, the other is RJ45. 
 
1.1.1 Connection method ( with RS232 ) 
- As of Figure 1-1, connect  RS232-In(9Pin) to Personal Computer,  
connect the next TV of Display to be connected from RS232-Out (9Pin). 
- In doing so, each device can be given from 0 to 253. 
  (Depends on the product actual range can be differ)  
- ID cannot be given duplicated. 
- When granting ID, it does not need to be given out in the connecting order. 
  
 
        Figure1-1  PC,TV or Monitor connecting method(with RS232) 
  

1.1.2 Connecting method(with RJ45) 
- There are several ways to connect Personal Computer and TV(or Monitor). 
- As of Figure 1-2, connect Hub and Personal Computer(using Ethernet).  
Connect each TV of Display to be connected to the Hub. 
- In doing so, each TV or Monitor must have an IP address. 
- TV or Monitor connected by protocol’s IP address must have the same ID with the protocol’s ID. 
- Each TV or Monitor ID can be duplicated. 
  
  
  Figure1-2  PC,TV or Monitor connecting method(with RJ45) 
  

1.1.3 Connecting method(with RJ45 & RS232C) 
- As of Figure 1-3, connect TV and Personal Computer(using Ethernet),  
connect the next TV of Display to be connected from RS232-Out (9Pin). 
- In doing so, only TV(connected to Personal Computer) needs an IP address.  
And each device ID can be given from 0 to 253. 
- ID cannot be given duplicated. 
- When granting ID, it does not need to be given out in the connecting order. 
  
 
Figure1-3  PC,TV or Monitor connecting method(with RJ45 & RS232C) 
  

1.2. Connection Spec 
1.2.1 RS232 Connection 
- Interactive communications using RS232. 
- Of RS232 standards, three signals RxD(No.2), TxD(No.3) and GND(No.5) are used 
→ Refer to Figure 2-1 
- Limit the distance between devices to less than 4m.  
- Currently, out of 9 PIN RS232 terminal, PINS in use are numbers 2, 3 and 5. 
- ID should show hexadecimal value of assigned ID. 
- If you want to control every mechanism connected with Serial Cable regardless of its ID,  
set ID part to “0xFE” and send commands. At the time, each SET will follow commands  
but it will not respond with ACK. 
 
Table 2-1  RS232 Network spec 
Bits Rate 9600 bps 
Data Bits 8 bits 
Parity None 
Stop Bits 1 bit 
Flow Control None 
  
  
Figure 2-1 RS-232 pin out DB-9 pin used for Asynchronous Data 
  

1.2.2 RJ45 Connection 
- Interactive communications using RJ45. 
- Transmit the MDC protocol using TCP/IP Format. The protocol information is stored in data area. 
- The protocol information format is the same as RS232’s. 
example) Power Off & ID=0 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Data1 
Checksum 
0xAA 0x11 1 Power 
TCP UDP 
IP ICMP ARP RARP 
Hardware Interface(Ethernet, PPP etc. ) 
→ 
Header Command 
0xFE 
Data Length Data1 
10 
0xAA 0x11 1 0 
TCP UDP 
IP ICMP ARP RARP 
Hardware Interface(Ethernet, PPP etc. ) 
- default ip : 192.168.0.10 PORT : 1515 
- The RJ45 plug has 8-Pins as below. 
Table 2-2  RJ45 plug 8-Pins 
RJ45 PIN# Wire Color(T568A) 10Base-T Signal 
100Base-TX Signal 1000Base-T Signal 
1 White/Green Transmit+ BI_DA+ 
2 Green Transmit- BI_DA- 
3 White/Orange Receive+ BI_DB+ 
4 Blue Unused BI_DC+ 
5 White/Blue Unused BI_DC- 
6 Orange Receive- BI_DB- 
7 White/Brown Unused BI_DD+ 
8 Brown Unused BI_DD- 
  
1.3 Protocol 
1.3.1 Packet Format 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Data 1 
Check Sum 
0xAA 0x11 1 Power 
. Header : Fixed Data 0xAA 
   . Command : Command data for each functionality.  
                Each command detail description is on Section 2. Command. 
   . ID : Which is set on command receiving device. 
        If the ID is not matched received command will be ignored. 
      * Broadcast Set :  
- ID 0xFE is used as broadcast set. 
If a certain device receive MDC packet which has ID 0xFE  
then device should handle that command 
In this case device will not make a reply for a broadcast set 
* Special ID(0xFF) : 
- If a certain device which has ID 0 receives command with ID 0xFF  
then ID 0 device needs to handle it and reply the ID as 0xFF 
   . Data Length : Data length of followed data. It is not include Check Sum 
   . Data1~N : Data Payload of each command 
               Each data payload is described on Section 2. Command 
   . Check Sum : Made by each data sum except Header and Check Sum itself. 
                 Discard the summation result which is over 256. 
       Example) Power On & ID=FE 
 Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Data 1 
Check Sum 
0xAA 0x11 1 Power 
→ The summation is 11+FE+01+01=111.  
Discard the overfolowed 256 so the check sum data is 11 
Header Command 
0xFE 
Data Length Data 1 
0x11 
0xAA 0x11 1 1 
 
  
1.3.2 Secure / Non Secure Connection on RJ45 Connection 
1.3.2.1 Non Secure Connection Workflow 
 
1.3.2.2 Secure Connection Workflow 
 
1) Client request the connection, Server accept the connection and send  
an unencrypted pre-handshake packet MDCSTART<<TLS>>. 
2) Device use self-signed OpenSSL certificate for TLS negotiation process with client.  
3) Client use the local copy of server certificate to verify and trust TLS session. 
 

4) Based on the server pre-handshake packet further TLS negotiation will be carried out. 
5) For authentication simple ASCII text message will be used of  
the format MDCAUTH<<Device_PIN>>. 
6) Server will reply Pass message as MDCAUTH<<PASS>> after successful pin verification.  
7) On failed pin verification, server will reply Fail message with three type of Error Codes (0xEC)  :
 MDCAUTH<<FAIL:0x00>> : for external error 
 MDCAUTH<<FAIL:0x01>> : for incorrect PIN 
 MDCAUTH<<FAIL:0x02>> : for incorrect PIN and retry count reached to 5 
8) After 5 failed attempts of PIN verification, server will stop verifying more attempts for the client 
application and will reply MDCAUTH<<FAIL:0x02>> for all next attempts. 
9) Fresh connection attempt can be made, after the server is restarted (i.e., device is rebooted).  
  
 
2. Command 
 
[Note] 
 1. If a certain field is not supported by product spec, 
    For set functionality, incoming data will be ignored 
    For get functionality, not supported field will be return as 0xff and  
if it is not available to sue 0xff for not supported it will be descrived on each command  
 
 2. Err code on NAK reply. 
    Error code data is used for internal purpose and can be differ by command and model.

2.1 Common Protocol 
2.1.00 Status Control 
● Function 
Get the device various state like power, volume, sound mute, input source, picture aspect ratio, timer 
  
● Get 
 Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Check 
Sum 0xAA 0x00 0x00 
 
● Set 
  Not Support 
 
● Ack 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack/Nak r-CMD Val 1 Val 2 
0xAA 0xFF 0x09 ‘A’ 0x00 Power Volume 
Val 3 Val 4 Val 5 Val 6 Val 7 Check 
Sum Mute Input Aspect N Time NF F Time NF 
  Power : Power code to be set on Device 
Volume : Volume value code ( 0 ~ 100 ) to be set on Device 
Mute : Mute code to be set on Device 
Input : Input Source code to be set on TV/Monitor 
Aspect : Image Size code to be set on TV/Monitor 
Note :   
1. If use New Timer (0xA4, 0xA5, 0xA6, 0xA7, 0xA8, 0xA9) command. Do as below. 
N Time NF : OnTime ON/OFF value of time to set TV/Monitor(old type Timer)  
F Time NF : OffTime ON/OFF value of time to set TV/Monitor(old type Timer) 
→ It was supported for old type Timer.  Now, It is always 0x00. 
      2. For no audio model volume and mute will be return as 0xff. 
 
● Nak 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack/Nak r-CMD Val 1 Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xFF 3 ‘N’ 0x00 ERR 
ERR : Error code that shows what occurred error is 
  
2.1.04 Video Control 
● Function 
Get the device picture settings like contrast, brightness, sharpness, color, tint, color tone, color temp  
  
● Working Condition 
1. ATV, DTV, AV, S-Video, Component, HDMI Only 
2. A product which has **** Text , **** Video/Image and Calibration as picture mode,  
It will not affected by the 1st condition and instead,  
It will be work with **** Video/Image of picture mode in the menu 
 
● Get 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Check 
Sum 0xAA 0x04 0x00 
 
● Set 
  Not Support 
 
● Ack 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack/Nak r-CMD Val 1 Val 2 
0xAA 0xFF 0x0A ‘A’ 0x04 Contrast Brightness 
Val 3 Val 4 Val 5 Val 6 Val 7 Val 8 Check 
Sum Sharpness Color Tint ColorTone ColorTemp 0 
Contrast : Contrast value to set the Device (0 ~ 100) 
Brightness : Brightness value to set the Device (0 ~ 100) 
Sharpness : Sharpness value to set the Device (0 ~ 100) 
Color : Color value to set the Device (0 ~ 100) 
Tint : Tint value to set the Device (0 ~ 100) 
Color Tone : Color Tone value to set the Device 
ColorTemp : Color Temperature value to set the Device  
 
● Nak 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack/Nak r-CMD Val 1 Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xFF 0x03 ‘N’ 0x04 ERR 
ERR : Error code that shows what occurred error is 
  
2.1.06 RGB Control 
● Function 
Get the device picture settings like contrast, brightness, color tone, color temperature, red gain, 
green gain, blue gain 
  
● Working Condition 
1. PC, BNC, DVI Only 
(On the DVI source Red, Green, Blue Gainwill not work) 
r. A product which has **** Text , **** Video/Image and Calibration as picture mode,  
It will not affected by the 1st condition and instead,  
It will be work with **** Text of picture mode in the menu 
 
● Get 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Check 
Sum 0xAA 0x06 0x00 
  
● Set 
  Not Support 
 
● Ack 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack/Nak r-CMD Val 1 Val 2 
0xAA 0xFF 0x0A ‘A’ 0x06 Contrast Brightness 
Val 3 Val 4 Val 5 Val 6 Val 7 Val 8 Check 
Sum ColorTone ColorTemp 0 Red Gain Green Gain Blue Gain 
  Val 1 ~ Val 8 : Same as above 
Note : If LFD model doesn’t support RGB Gain, those values should be replied with 0xFF.  
If then MDC application can ignore these values. 
  
● Nak 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack/Nak r-CMD Val 1 Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xFF 0x03 ‘N’ 0x06 ERR 
ERR : Error code that shows what occurred error is 
  
2.1.07 PIP Status Control 
● Function 
Get the device status of PIP related things like pip size, pip source 
 
● Get 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Check 
Sum 0xAA 0x07 0x00 
 
● Set 
  Not Support 
 
● Ack 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack/Nak r-CMD Val 1 Val 2 
0xAA 0xFF 0x06 ‘A’ 0x07 P.Size P.Source 
Val 3 Val 4 Check 
Sum 0 0 
 P.Size : The PIP size code set for the TV or monitor. 
  Note : For the detail, pls refer 0x42 PIP Size control command 
P.Source : The PIP source code set for the TV or monitor. 
  
● Nak 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack/Nak r-CMD Val 1 Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xFF 0x03 ‘N’ 0x07 ERR 
 ERR : The error code indicating which error occurred. 
  
2.1.08 Maintenance Control

Power : Power code set on Device 
P.Size : PIP Size value code set on Device 
P.Source : PIP Source value code set on Device 
Note : In case of PIP source is not valid status, till 2018 year model it will return as 0x00 and from 
the 2019year model it will return as 0xff 
Lmax_H : Auto Lamp Max Time Hour (1 ~ 12) set on Device 
Lmax_M : Auto Lamp Max Time Minute (0 ~ 59) set on Device 
Lmax_AP : Auto Lamp Max Time AM/PM set on Device 
LmaxValue : Auto Lamp Max value (0 ~ 100) set on Device 
Lmin_H : Auto Lamp Min Time Hour (1 ~ 12) set on Device 
Lmin_M : Auto Lamp Min Time Minute (0 ~ 59) set on Device 
Lmin_AP : Auto Lamp Min Time AM/PM set on Device 
LminValue : Auto Lamp Min value (0 ~ 100, 0xFF) set on Device 
LampValue : Manual Lamp Control value (0 ~ 100, 0xFF) set on Device 
ScreenInterval : Safety Screen Interval (Per Hour, 0(0ff)~10) set on Device 
ScreenTime : Safety Screen Time (Per Second, 0(off) ~5) set on Device 
ScreenType : SBP Type Code set on Device 
0x00 OFF 0x00 OFF 
0x01   0x81   
0x02   0x82

(Timer : Repeat) 0x83 Scroll 
(Timer : Interval)

(Timer : Repeat) 0x84 Pixel 
(Timer : Interval)

(Timer : Repeat) 0x86 Eraser 
(Timer : Interval)

(Timer : Repeat) 0x89 All White 
(Timer : Interval)

(Timer : Repeat) 0x8A Pattern 
(Timer : Interval) 
…   …   
0x10 Rolling Bar 
(Timer : Repeat) 0x90 Rolling Bar 
(Timer : Interval) 
0x11 Fading Screen 
(Timer : Repeat) 0x91 Fading Screen 
(Timer : Interval) 
Note : Bit 7 means timer type is interval or repeat one.  
If the bit7 is 1 then it means a interval type timer and if it is 0 then it means a repeat type timer  
  Start Time-Hour : Start Time Hour value ( 1 ~ 12 ) 
Start Time-Min : Start Time Minute value ( 0 ~ 59 ) 
Start Time-am/pm : Start Time AM/PM ( 0 ~ 1 ), 1 : AM, 0 : PM 
End Time-Hour : Start Time Hour value ( 1 ~ 12 ) 
End Time-Min : Start Time Minute value ( 0 ~ 59 ) 
End Time-am/pm : Start Time AM/PM ( 0 ~ 1 ), 1 : AM, 0 : PM 
V.Wall : code set on Device 
V.WallFormat : Video Wall Format code set on Device 
V.WallDivid : Video Wall Divider code set on Device 
V.WallSet : Video f Set Number code set on Device 
Note : If LminValue is returned to 0xFF then Auto Lamp Control is OFF. 
If LampValue is returned to 0xFF then Manual Lamp Control is OFF. 
         If videlwall related field returned as 0xFF then videowall is not suooprted

Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack/Nak r-CMD Val 1 Val 2 
0xAA 0xFF 0x0D ‘A’ 0x09 Vol Balance 
Val 3 Val 4 Val 5 Val 6 Val 7 Val 8 Val 9 Val 10 
100Hz 300Hz 1kHz 3kHz 10kHz 0 0 0 
Val 11 Check 
Sum SRS 
Vol, Balance : Vol, Balance value set on Device 
100Hz, 300Hz, 1kHz, 3kHz, 10kHz : Each the frequency of the Equalizer value set on Device 
The mean value is 0x0A. Value range is 0 ~ 20. In LFD menu it varies from -10 to +10. 
menu 0 value is 0x0a  
menu -10 is 0x00 
SRS : SRS TSXT On/Off value set on Device 
 
[Type 2] 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack/Nak r-CMD Val 1 Val 2 
0xAA 0xFF 0x0C ‘A’ 0x09 Vol Balance 
Val 3 Val 4 Val 5 Val 6 Val 7 Val 8 Val 9 Val 10 
100Hz 200Hz 500Hz 1kHz 2kHz 5kHz 10kHz SRS 
Check 
Sum 
Vol, Balance : Vol, Balance value set on Device 
100Hz, 200Hz, 500Hz, 1kHz, 2kHz, 5kHz, 10kHz : Each the frequency of the Equalizer value set on 
device. The mean value is 0x0A. Value range is 0 ~ 20. Menu item 0 is matched with 0x0a on this 
command and menu item -10 is 0 as same 
SRS : SRS TSXT On/Off value on device

e Error 
Val 3 Val 4 Val 5 Val 6 
Check 
Sum Bright_Sens
or Error 
No_Sync 
Error  Cur_Temp FAN Error 
   Lamp Error : Lamp Error code (0 : Normal, 1 : Error) to be set on Device  
Temperature Error : Temperature Error code (0: Normal, 1: Error) to be set on Device 
Bright_Sensor Error : Brighte Sensor Error code (0: NONE, 1: Error, 2: NORMAL) to be set on 
TV/Monitor  
No_Sync Error 
0x00 Normal 0x01 Error, No Sync 
0x02 Not Available 0x03 Not Connected 
Note : Invalid status will be replied when current source is app source 
       Error status will be replied with input signal of not supported resolution or no signal 
       “Not Connected” will support by product spec 
Cur_Temp : Current temperature of Device (-60℃ ~ 125℃) 
Note : If there any read fail, temp value will be return as 0xff 
       Actual temperature range will be differ by each product spec 
FAN Error 
0x00 Normal 0x01 Error 
0x02 Fan is not supported - - 
Note : If any data field is returned as 0xff, means it is invalid one 
        Based on the product spec, this command replay can be over 1sec.

Header Command

0x00 Power OFF 0x01 Power ON 
0x02 Reboot 
  
● Ack 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack/Nak r-CMD Val 1 Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xFF 0x03 ‘A’ 0x11 Power 
Power : Same as above 
  
● Nak 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack/Nak r-CMD Val 1 Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xFF 0x03 ‘N’ 0x11 ERR 
  ERR : Error code that shows what occurred error is 
Note :  
- When you execute power on function by RJ45 MDC then you must re-connect  
        a socket connection after 10 sec. 
   - When Monitor is Power Off status and connect by RJ45 Then you must transmit the WOL  
protocol instead of MDC protocol using TCP/IP Format for Power On.  
(In “Network Standby : Off” Condition(DMD/DBD/DHD/UED/DMD-S)  
and always (Other Models) 
- If you send a MDC Command for “PowerOn” or “PowerOff” 
It must retry for 3 times every 2 Seconds until ACK command.  
If there is no ACK within 3 times, It means failure. 
 
Please refer below explanation  
S) SET POWER OFF 
0xAA,0x11,0x01,0x00,0x0x12    :  MONITOR 1 
0xAA,0x11,0x02,0x00,0x0x13    :  MONITOR 2 
0xAA,0x11,0x01,0x00,0x0x12    :  MONITOR 1 
0xAA,0x11,0x02,0x00,0x0x13    :  MONITOR 2 
0xAA,0x11,0x01,0x00,0x0x12    :  MONITOR 1 
0xAA,0x11,0x02,0x00,0x0x13    :  MONITOR 2 
  
2) SET POWER ON 
0xAA,0x11,0x01,0x01,0x0x13    :  MONITOR 1 
0xAA,0x11,0x02,0x01,0x0x14    :  MONITOR 2 
0xAA,0x11,0x01,0x01,0x0x13    :  MONITOR 1 
0xAA,0x11,0x02,0x01,0x0x14    :  MONITOR 2 
0xAA,0x11,0x01,0x01,0x0x13    :  MONITOR 1 
0xAA,0x11,0x02,0x01,0x0x14    :  MONITOR 2

Header Command 
ID

0xAA 0xFF 0x0A ‘A’ 0x17 Country ATV_DTV

(Hgh)

Country : Select the country to be set on Device (0 : Korea, 1: USA, …. ) 
ATV_DTV : Select Analog TV and DTV to be set on Device ( 0 : Analog TV, 1: Digital TV) 
AirCalbe : Select if TV is cabled or general ( 0 : general, 1: cabled) 
CH_NUM : TV channel number to be set on Device ( Analog TV :  1 ~ 135 ,  Digital TV : 0 ~ 999) 
Sel_Minor : Select minor channel when DTV is to be set on Device 
( 0 : minor channel not selected. 1: minor channel selected.) 
Minor_CH : Select minor channel number when DTV is to be set on Device( 0 ~ 999.)

0xAA 0x1B 0x04 0xA2 Week Day Time Min 
 Check 
Sum 
Week Day 
Bit7 Bit6 Bit5 Bit4 Bit3 Bit2 Bit1 Bit0 
Reserved Monday Tuesday Wendesda
y Thursday Friday Saturday Sunday 
Monday ~ Sunday : 0 – Do not restart, 1 – Do restart 
Time : Restart time by hour (0 ~ 23), 0xff means invalid data 
Min : Restart time by min (0 ~ 59), 0xff means invalid data

2.1.28 Tint Control 
● Function 
Control the device tint. Adjust the ratio of green to red tint level 
 
● Working Condition 
1. AV, S-Video, Component, DVI(HDCP) Only 
2. A product which has **** Text , **** Video/Image and Calibration as picture mode,  
it will not affected by the 1st condition and instead,  
It will be work with **** Video/Image of picture mode in the menu 
 
● Get 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Check 
Sum 0xAA 0x28 0x00 
  
● Set 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Data 1 Check 
Sum 0xAA 0x28 0x01 Tint 
Tint : Tint value code to be set on TV/Monitor (0 ~ 100 ) 
      . 0 means most green sided 
      . 50 means neutral between green and red 
      . 100 means most red sided 
Note : Depends on the product spec, tint could only be set in 50 Steps (0, 2, 4, 6… 100) 
  
● Ack 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack/Nak r-CMD Val 1 Check

32(0x20) 3200K 105(0x69) 10500K

50(0x32) 5000K 125(0x7d) 12500K 
55(0x37) 5500K 130(0x82) 13000K 
60(0x3c) 6000K 135(0x87) 13500K 
65(0x41) 6500K 140(0x8c) 14000K 
70(0x46) 7000K 145(0x91) 14500K 
75(0x4b) 7500K 150(0x96) 15000K 
80(0x50) 8000K 155(0x9b) 15500K 
85(0x55) 8500K 160(0xa0) 16000K 
90(0x5a) 9000K

2.1.4C Pixel Shift Control  
● Function 
Control the device pixel shift of screen burn protection function 
Note : If video wall is on, zoom is on or input signal is vesa format on DVI source then it will not work

Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Check

Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Data 1 Data 2 Data 3 Data 4 
0xAA 0x4C 0x04 Shift H.Dot V.Line S.Time 
Check 
Sum 
Shift : Pixel Shift On/Off Code to be set on TV/Monitor 
Note : If Shift value is off, H.Dot, V.Line, S.Time values are ignored in Device. 
0x00 OFF 0x01 ON 
H.Dot : Horizontal Dot value code set on TV/Monitor (0 ~ 4) 
V.Line : Vertical Line value code set on TV/Monitor (0 ~ 4) 
S.Time : Shift Time value code set on TV/Monitor (1 ~ 4)

2.1.57 Auto Lamp Control 
● Function 
Control the device lamp schedule 
Note :When Manual Lamp Control is on, Auto Lamp Control will automatically turn off. 
  
● Get 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Check 
Sum 0xAA 0x57 0x00 
  
● Set 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Data 1 Data 2 Data 3 Data 4 
0xAA 0x57 0x08 Lmax_H Lmax_M Lmax_AP LmaxValue 
Data 5 Data 6 Data 7 Data 8 Check 
Sum Lmin_H Lmin_M Lmin_AP LminValue 
Lmax_H : Auto Lamp Max Time Hour set on TV/Monitor (1 ~ 12) 
Lmax_M : Auto Lamp Max Time Minute set on TV/Monitor (0 ~ 59) 
Lmax_AP : Auto Lamp Max Time set on TV/Monitor AM/PM (AM :1 / PM:0) 
LmaxValue : Auto Lamp Max Value set on TV/Monitor (0 ~ 100) 
Lmin_H : Auto Lamp Min Time Hour set on TV/Monitor (1 ~ 12) 
Lmin_M : Auto Lamp Min Time Minute set on TV/Monitor (0 ~ 59) 
Lmin_AP : Auto Lamp Min Time set on TV/Monitor AM/PM (AM :1 / PM:0) 
LminValue : Auto Lamp Min Value set on TV/Monitor (0 ~ 100) 
Note  :  When LminValue is returned to 0xFF, Auto Lamp Control is off. 
When Dynamic contrast is On, Auto Lamp Control does not operate. 
  
● Ack 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack/Nak r-CMD Val 1 Val 2 
0xAA 0xFF 0x0A ‘A’ 0x57 Lmax_H Lmax_M 
Val 3 Val 4 Val 5 Val 6 Val 7 Val 8 Check 
Sum Lmax_AP LmaxValue Lmin_H Lmin_M Lmin_AP LminValue 
Lmax_H, Lmax_M, Lmax_AP, LmaxValue, Lmin_H, Lmin_M, Lmin_AP, LminValue : Same as above  
  
● Nak 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack/Nak r-CMD Val 1 Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xFF 3 ‘N’ 0x57 ERR 
ERR : Error code that shows what occurred error is

2.1.5B Safety Screen Control 
● Function 
Control the device safety screen timer 
 
● Get 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Check 
Sum 0xAA 0x5B 0x00 
 
● Set 
[Mode 1] When the Timer is Repeat 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Data 1 Data 2 Data 3 Check 
Sum 0xAA 0x5B 0x03 Type T.Period T.Time 
[Mode 2] When the Timeris Interval 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Data 1 Data 2 Data 3 Data 4 
0xAA 0x5B 0x07 Type StartTime- 
Hour 
StartTime-
Min. 
StartTime-
am/pm 
Data 5 Data 6 Data 7 
Check 
Sum EndTime 
-Hour 
EndTime 
-Min. 
EndTime 
-am/pm 
Type :Timer type to set Device 
Timer Type Data for Repeat Data for Interval 
OFF 0x00 0x00 
Scroll 0x03 0x83 
Pixel 0x04 0x84 
Bar 0x05 0x85 
Eraser 0x06 0x86 
All White 0x09 0x89 
Pattern 0x0A 0x8A 
Rolling Bar 0x10 0x90 
Fading Screen 0x11 0x91 
Note : 
- If the value is 0x00, means timer is off.(It dosen’t matter the length 3/7) 
- If the value is not 0x00 and the MSB is 00 means timer type is Repeat  
and the MSB is 1 means timer type is interval 
- All White, Pattern are only work with PDP model 
T.Period : Timer periode hour data to set Device (1 ~ 10 Hr.) 
T.Time :Timer periode code to set Device (10 ~ 50 sec.) 
0x01 10 sec 
0x02 20 sec 
0x03 30 sec 
0x04 40 sec 
0x05 50 sec 
Note : If the timer type is Rolling Bar or Fading Screen, timer will work only 1 cycleregardless it’s type 
      If the timer periode is 0 or timer time is 0, timer will turn off 
 (IF the timer type is Rolling Bar or Fading Scree it will not turns off) 
Start Time-Hour : The value of Start Time Hour (1 ~ 12) 
Start Time-Min : The value of Start Time Minute ( 0 ~ 59 ) 
Start Time-am/pm : The value of Start Time AM/PM (1 : AM, 0 : PM)  
End Time-Hour : The value of End Time Hour ( 1 ~ 12 ) 
End Time-Min : The value of End Time Minute 값 ( 0 ~ 59 ) 
End Time-am/pm : The value of End Time AM/PM (1 : AM, 0 : PM) 
  
● Ack 
[Mode 1] When the Timer is Repeat

ID

Val 3 Check 
Sum T.Time

ID

Note : Based on the product spec, each option will work or not 
Length : It means the variable length of data that is going to be sent. 
You can set it differently depending on the length of message data and you need to input 
messages according to length that already set.  
Ticker On/Off :Ticker’s On/Off Code that is going to be set in Device( 0 ~ 1 ) 
0x00 Ticker Off 0x01 Ticker On 
Start Hour : The value of Start Time Hour that operate Ticker in Device ( 1 ~ 12 ) 
Strat Minute :  The value of Start Time Minute that operate Ticker in Device ( 0 ~ 59 ) 
Start AM/PM : Start Time AM/PM that operate Ticker in Device( 0 ~ 1 ) 
0x00 PM 0x01 AM 
End Hour : The value of End Time Hour that operate Ticker in Device( 1 ~ 12 ) 
End Minute : The value of End Time Minute that operate Ticker in Device ( 0 ~ 59 ) 
End AM/PM : End Time AM/PM that operate Ticker in Device( 0 ~ 1 ) 
0x00 PM 0x01 AM 
Position Horizontal : Value of horizontal position of message that is presented in Device (0 ~ 2) 
Position Vertical : The value of vertical position of message that is presented in Device ( 0 ~ 2 ) 
Position Horizontal Position Vertical 
0x00 Center 0x00 Middle 
0x01 Left 0x01 Top 
0x02 Right 0x02 Bottom 
Motion On/Off : On/Off Code of Motion that is set in Device ( 0 ~ 1 ) 
0x00 Motion Off 0x01 Motion On 
Motion Direction : The direction which motion that is set in Device moves ( 0 ~ 3 ) 
0x00 Left 0x01 Right 
0x02 Up 0x03 Down 
Motion Speed : The speed which motion that is set in Device moves ( 0 ~ 2 ) 
Font Size : The font size of message that is set in Device ( 0 ~ 2 ) 
Motion Speed Font Size 
Normal 0x00 Standard 0x00 
Slow 0x01 Small 0x01 
Fast 0x02 Large 0x02 
Foreground Color : Foreground Color of message that is set in Device ( 0 ~ 7 ) 
Background Color : Background Color of message that is set in Device ( 0 ~ 7 ) 
Foreground Color Background Color 
0x00 Black 0x00 Black 
0x01 White 0x01 White 
0x02 Red 0x02 Red 
0x03 Green 0x03 Green 
0x04 Blue 0x04 Blue 
0x05 Yellow 0x05 Yellow 
0x06 Magenta 0x06 Magenta 
0x07 Cyan 0x07 Cyan 
Foreground Opacity : Foreground Opacity of message that is set in Device ( 0 ~ 3 ) 
Background Opacity : Background Opacity of message that is set in Device ( 0 ~ 3 ) 
Foreground Opacity Background Opacity 
0x03 Flashing 0x00 Solid  
0x04 Flash All 0x01 Transparent 
0x05 Off 0x02 Translucent 
   Message Data : Enter Ticker Message that is displayed in Device.  
It is sent as hexadecimal value of message and it can be entered up to 232 bytes 
Ex) Hello => 0x48 0x65 0x6C 0x6C 0x6F 
Note : Based on the product spec, it is supported multi lingual with UTF8 format and more than 25    
characters 
Font Style Reset : If font size reset is chosen in MDC Application, all values from Data 13 to Data 17  
 will be 0x00 and Set command is sent to get Default value.

Note :

2.1.8B Video Wall Direct User Control 
● Function 
Control the device video wall related things like On/Off, mode, whole screen division, device number 
and input 
Note : This does not operate while PIP is operating. 
 
● Get 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Check 
Sum 0xAA 0x8B 0x00 
 
● Set 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Data 1 Data 2 Data 3 Data 4 
0xAA 0x8B 0x05 V.Wall_On WallMode Wall_Div Wall_Sno 
Data 5 Check 
Sum Input 
V.Wall_On: The Video Wall code to set for the TV or monitor. 
0x00 Video Wall OFF 0x01 Video Wall ON 
WallMode: The Video Wall mode code to set for the TV or monitor. 
0x00 Natural 0x01 Full 
Wall_Div: The Video Wall Divider code set for the TV or monitor. 
- Please refer Wall_Div table of Command 0x89, Video Wall User Control 
Wall_Sno: The TV/Monitor serial number code set for the TV or monitor. 
- Please refer Wall_Sno table of Command 0x89, Video Wall User Control 
Input : The input source code to set for the TV or monitor. 
           - Please refer Input table of Command 0x14, Input Source & App Control (MFM).

2.1.A3 OSD Display Type On/Off 
● Function 
Control the device OSD mode for a specified category 
Note : “OSD On” means, Display OSD which is set on OSD Type. 
“OSD Off” means, Does not display which is set on OSD Type. 
 
● Get 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xA3 0x00 
 
● Set 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Data 1 Data 2 
Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xA3 0x02 OSD 
Type 
OSD 
On/Off 
OSD Type: Select OSD Type code to be set on TV/Monitor 
0x00 Source OSD 0x01 Not Optimum Mode OSD 
0x02 No Signal OSD 0x03 MDC OSD 
0x04 Schedule Channel Info - - 
Note : Depends on the product “0x04 Schedule Channel Info” is worked as Download Satus Message 
OSD ON/OFF: Adjust OSD On/Off code to be set on TV/Monitor 
0x00 OSD Off 0x01 OSD On

Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack/Nak r-CMD Val1

2.1.A7 Clock Control_MFM 
● Function 
Control the device clock as day, hour, min, month year and AM/PM 
Note : Depends on the produce spec it will work 
       Similar command 0xc5 is exist 
 
● Get 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xA7 0x00 
 
● Set 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Data 1 Data 2 Data 3 Data 4 
0xAA 0xA7 0x07 Day H Time M Time Month 
Data 5 Data 6 Data 7 Check 
Sum Year1 Year2 AP Time 
Day : Day value to be set on TV/Monitor ( 1 ~ 31 ) 
Month : Month value to be set on TV/Monitor ( 1 ~ 12 ) 
Year1 : Year value to be set on TV/Monitor (High Byte) 
Year2 : Year value to be set on TV/Monitor (Low Byte) 
ex) Current year is 2010. 
    2010(Dec) → 0x07DA(Hex)  => Year1: 0x07, Year2: 0xDA 
Hour  : Hour value to be set on TV/Monitor ( 1 ~ 12 ) 
Minute : Minute value to be set on TV/Monitor ( 0 ~ 59 ) 
AmPm  :  AM/PM value to be set on TV/Monitor (0 ~ 1) 
0x00 PM 0x01 AM 
 
● Ack 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack/Nak r-CMD Val 1 Val 2 
0xAA 0xFF 0x09 ‘A’ 0xA7 Day H Time 
Val 3 Val 4 Val 5 Val 6 Val 7 Check 
Sum M Time Month Year1 Year2 AP Time 
Val 1 ~ Val 7 : Same as above 
Note : Hour, Minute if current time was not set on Monitor, 0xFF 
 
● Nak 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack/Nak r-CMD Val 1 Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xFF 0x03 ‘N’ 0xA7 ERR 
ERR : Error code that shows what occurred error is 
  
2.1.A8 Holiday Add/Delete Control 
● Function 
Add/Delete the device holiday schedule with the holiday schedule itself start month/day and end 
month/day 
 
● Get 
  Not Support 
 
● Set 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Data 1 Data 2 Data 3 Data 4 
0xAA 0xA8 0x05 
Manageme
nt 
command 
Month1 Day1 Month2 
Data 5 Check 
Sum Day2 
Management Command: Adjust Command  Holiday List of Device. 
0x00 Add Holiday  
0x01 Delete Holiday 
0x02 Delete All 
Note :  
- If param is Delete All, Data 2 ~ Data 5 must be set 0. 
- Add Holiday : Add New Holiday Information “Month1/Day1 ~ Month2/Day2”. 
- Delete Holiday : Delete one Holiday Information “Month1/Day1 ~ Month2/Day2”. 
- Delete All : Delete All Holiday Information.(“Data2 ~ Data5” must be 0x00.)

command

2.1.A9 Holiday Get Control 
● Function

Note : Depends on the spec it will be work 
. 
● Get  
  [Total Number of Holiday]

ID

[Each holiday schedule] 
Request each holiday schedule 
Header Command 
ID

Index :  Index value on Holiday List. 
  
● Set  
  Not Support 
 
● Ack 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack/Nak r-CMD Val 1 Val 2 
0xAA 0xFF 0x07 ‘A’ 0xA9 Index Month1 
Val 3 Val 4 Val 5 Check 
Sum Day1 Month2 Day2 
When the value of Val 2 ~ Val 5 is 0, “Get Holiday” is an ACK, Val 1 is number of Holiday information 
set on TV/Monitor 
When the value of Val 2 ~ Val 5 is 0xFF, requested information of index that doesn ’t set holiday. 
 
Rule of Ack Command. 
Input Type Index Month 1 Day 1 Month 2 Day 2 
Get Number of Holiday Total 
number  0 0 0 0 
Index which is set  
Holiday Set Index 
Month1

data) 
Day1 
(Index’s 
data)

(Index’s 
data)

(Index’s 
data)

DST On/Off : DST Value 
Tunerless Model Tuner supported Model 
0x00 DST Off 0x00 DST Off 
0x01 --  0x01 Auto 
0x02 DST On 0x02 Manual 
Note : Data2 ~12 are valid in case of DST On or Manual 
Month of Start Date, Month of End Date : Month in which DST start/end (0x00 : Jan ~ 0x0b : Dec) 
Week Info of Start Date, Week Info of End Date : Order of the day of the week in which DST 
start/end.  
0x00 1st 0x01 2nd 
0x02 3rd 0x03 4th 
0x04 Last   
Weekday Info of Start Date, Weekday Info of End Date : Day of week in which DST start/end (0x00 : 
Mon ~ 0x06 : Sun) 
Time H of Start date, Time H of End date : Hours of the time that DST start/end (0 ~ 23) 
Time M of Start date, Time M of End date : Minutes of the time that DST start/end (0 ~ 59) 
Time Off Set : Value of Time offset 
0x00 +1:00 0x01 +2:00

2.1.B7 Custom PIP Control 
● Function 
Control the device custom PIP related things like horizontal/vertical position and horizontal/vertical 
size 
Note : It update custom PIP related things and when PIP mode is set as cusom it will work 
   
● Get 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xB7 0x00 
 
● Set  
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Data 1 Data 2 Data 3 Data 4 
0xAA 0xB7 0x08 H Position V Position 
Data 5 Data 6 Data 7 Data 8 Check 
Sum H Size V Size 
H Position : Custom PIP horizontal start position 
V Position : Custom PIP vertical start position 
H Size : Custom PIP horizontal size 
V Size : Custom PIP vertical size 
Note :  
- The PIP Start Position and Size can not over panel H, V size 
- H/V Size : 512 * 288 ~ 1632 * 918  (H Interval : 160 pixel, V Interval : 90 pixel) 
512*288, 672*378, 832*468, 992*558, 1152*648, 1312*738, 1472*828, 1632*918 
- H/V Position : Interval 10 Pixel 
   
● Ack 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack/Nak r-CMD Val 1 Val 2 
0xAA 0xFF 0x0A ‘A’ 0xB7 H Position 
Val 3 Val 4 Val 5 Val 6 Val 7 Val 8 Check 
Sum V Position H Size V Size 
H Position, V Position, H Size, V Size : Same as above

2.1.C3 Apply Calibrated data for All Source or Current Source 
● Function 
Control auto calibration result to all source or current only 
Note:  
- it will work on non ACM12 applied model 
- Depends on the product spec, it is matched with menu item Apply Picture Setting 
 
● Get 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xC3 0x00 
  Note : It will be supported or not based on product spec 
 
● Set 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Data 1 Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xC3 0x01 Apply 
Apply : Apply the auto calibration data to all source or current only 
0x00 Current input video source 0x01 All input video source 
 
● Ack 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack/Nak r-CMD Val 1 Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xFF 0x03 ‘A’ 0xC3 Apply  
Apply : Same as above 
 
● Nak 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack/Nak r-CMD Val 1 Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xFF 0x03 ‘N’ 0xC3 ERR 
ERR : Error Code which is displayed when error is ccurred. 
  
2.1.C5 Clock Control_MFM (Second field can be set) 
● Function 
Control the device clock as day, hour, min, month year and AM/PM 
Note : It will work on the signage device which is product after 13year 
Similar command 0xc5 is exist 
 
● Get 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xC5 0x00 
 
● Set 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Val 1 Val 2 Val 3 Val 4 
0xAA 0xC5 0x08 Day H Time M Time S Time 
Val 5 Val 6 Val 7 Val 8 Check 
Sum Month Year AP Time 
Day : Day value to be set on TV/Monitor ( 1 ~ 31 ) 
H Time : Hour value to be set on TV/Monitor ( 1 ~ 12 ) 
M Time : Minute value to be set on TV/Monitor ( 0 ~ 59 ) 
S Time : Second value to be set on TV/Monitor ( 0 ~ 59 ) 
Month : Month value to be set on TV/Monitor ( 1 ~ 12 ) 
Year : Year value to be set on TV/Monitor 
ex) Current year is 2010. 
    2010(Dec) → 0x07DA(Hex)  => Year1: 0x07, Year2: 0xDA  
AP Time :  AM/PM value to be set on TV/Monitor ( 0 ~ 1 ) 
0x00 PM 0x01 AM 
 
● Ack 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack/Nak r-CMD Val 1 Val 2 
0xAA 0xFF 0x0A ‘A’ 0xC5 Day H Time 
Val 3 Val 4 Val 5 Val 6 Val 7 Val 8 Check 
Sum M Time S Time Month Year AP Time 
Day, H Time, M Time, S Time, Month, Year, AP Time  : Same as above 
Note : Hour, Minute if current time was not set on device it will be 0xFF 
  
● Nak 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack/Nak r-CMD Val 1 Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xFF 0x03 ‘N’ 0xC5 ERR 
ERR : Error code that shows what occurred error is

Check

Off 
AutoPowerOff 
0x00 Off 0x01 4 Hour(On) 
0x02 6 Hour 0x03 8 Hour 
0x04 16 Hour - - 
  Note : If the model has On/Off value only, Data 0 is Off and Data 1 is On.

2.1.D0.92 Module WB (RGB) COntrol 
● Function 
  Control the LED module white balance 
 
● Get 
[Type1] 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Sub CMD Data1 
Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xD0 0x02 0x92 Module 
Info 
Module Info 
Bit7 Bit6 Bit5 Bit4 Bit3 Bit2 Bit1 Bit0 
Reset Module ID X Y 
Reset : Reset when data is 1 
Module ID : Modeule id of each cabinet 
X : Red = 0, Green = 1, Blue = 2, All Y Line = 3 
Y : Red = 0, Green = 1, Blue = 2, All X Line = 3 
Note : Ex) If (X,Y) = 3,2 , Set/Get RB, GB, BB 
If (X,Y) = 1,3 , Set/Get GR, GG, GB 
If Reset (bit7) is 1 and X/Y is 0x0F, currnet Module will be set as default on cabinet.  
Ex) 0x9F means module ID1 will be set as default value. 
(In case of type2 , Data1 is 0x81, Data2 is 0xff) 
If Module Info is 0xFF, All Modlues will be set as default on cabinet 
(In case of type2 , Data1 is 0xff, Data2 is 0xff)

and for cabinet diagnosis information gathering performance improving

ID

Note : Reply format will be differ based on the diagnosis info type

HDBT Status : Detail information is same with description of 0xD0 subcommand 0x84 
Temperature : Detail information is same with description of 0xD0 subcommand 0x84 
Illuminance : Detail information is same with description of 0xD0 subcommand 0x84 
Module N : Detail information is same with description of 0xD0 subcommand 0x84 
Module1 LED Error Data N : Detail information is same with description of 0xD0 subcommand 0x84

2.1.E0 Net PIP (MagicInfo Only) 
● Function 
  Control the device PIP related things like horizontal/vertical start position, horizontal/vertical size, 
source, channel, sound select, country, ATV/DTV, air/cable, ch num and minor ch num 
Note : 1. The possible PIP composition and PIP size depends on H/W spec.  
2. After Net PIP turns on, if user changes other sources and come back to Magicinfo,  
Net PIP also should be shown. 
   
● Get 
Not Support 
  
● Set 
[PIP On] 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length PIP ON Data 1 Data 2 Data 3 
0xAA 0xE0 0x14 0x01 H Position V Position 
High-Byte 
Data 4 Data 5 Data 6 Data 7 Data 8 Data 9 Data 10 Data 11 
V Position 
Low-Byte H Size V Size P.Source TV Channel S.Select 
Data 12 Data 13 Data 14 Data 15 Data 16 Data 17 Data 18 Data 19 
Country ATV/ 
DTV AirCable CH_NUM Sel_Minor Minor_CH 
Check 
Sum 
H Position : The Position value code for PIP H-Start 
V Position : The Position value code for PIP V-Start 
H Size : The Size value code for PIP H-width 
V Size : The Size value code for PIP V-width 
Note : The PIP Start Position and Size do not over panel H, V size 
P.Source : The input source code to set for the TV or monitor. 
           - Please refer Input table of Command 0x14, Input Source & App Control (MFM). 
TV Channel : Channel Number ( 0 ~ 99 )  
Note : 460Txn Only (Platform LFD don’t use this byte) 
S.Select : The Sound select Code 
0x00 MagicInfo Sound 0x01 PIP Sound 
Country : The value code for the country of the Device(0 : Korea, 1 : U.S.A, ...) 
ATV_DTV : The value code for the ATV/DTV of the Device(0 : Analog TV, 1 : Digital TV) 
AirCable : The value code for the Air/Cable of the Device(0 : Air, 1 : Cable) 
CH_NUM High_Byte : The value code for the Major Channel High-Byte of the TV / DTV 
(Analog TV : 1 ~ 135, Digital TV : 0 ~ 999) 
CH_NUM Low_Byte : The value code for the Major Channel Low-Byte of the TV / DTV 
(Analog TV : 1 ~ 135, Digital TV : 0 ~ 999) 
Sel_Minor : The value code for the Minor Channel Enable/Disable of the Device 
(0 : Enable, 1 : Disable)(DTV Only) 
Minor_CH High_Byte : The value code for the Minor Channel High-Byte of the TV / 
Monitor( 0 ~ 999 )(DTV Only) 
Minor_CH Low_Byte : The value code for the Minor Channel Low-Byte of the TV / 
Monitor( 0 ~ 999 )(DTV Only) 
Note : CH_NUM High_Byte = 0xFF, CH_NUM Low_Byte = 0xFF, Sel_Minor = 
0x01, Minor_CH High_Byte = 0xFF, Minor_CH Low_Byte = 0xFF  
=> Net PIP tune as last Memory channel of TV source 
 
 [PIP Off] 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length PIP Off Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xE0 0x01 0x00 
 
● Ack 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack/Nak r-CMD PIP ON Val 1 
0xAA 0xFF 0x16 ‘A’ 0xE0 0x01 H Position 
High -Byte 
Val 2 Val 3 Val 4 Val 5 Val 6 Val 7 Val 8 Val 9 
H Position 
Low -Byte V Position H Size V Size P.Source 
Val 10 Val 11 Val 12 Val 13 Val 14 Val 15 Val 16 Val 17 
TV Channel S.Select Country ATV_DTV AirCable CH_NUM Sel_Minor 
Val 18 Val 19 Check 
Sum Minor_CH 
Val 1 ~ Val 19 : Same as above 
 
● Nak 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack/Nak r-CMD Val 1 Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xFF 3 ‘N’ 0xE0 ERR 
ERR : Error Code which is displayed when error is 340ccurred.

2.1.FD Auto ID Setting MDC Control Command 
● Function 
  Communication data apth control for MDC auto ID functionality 
 
● Get 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xFD 0x00 
 
● Set 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Data 1 Data 2 Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xFD 0x02 RS_Status M_ID 
Note : If M_ID is 0, can’t chage ID. (previous value.) 
RS_Status : RS232 Output , ID information 
Bit7 Bit6 Bit5 Bit4 Bit3 Bit2 Bit1 Bit0 
0 0 0 1 or 0 0 0 0 1 or 0 
  1 : Initialize Monitor ID 
 (Initiailize Monitor ID to 0) 
 0 : - 
1 : RS232 Loop Out Disable 
 0 : RS232 Loop Out Enable 
Note : In Get Auto ID,can’t know Monitor ID’s reset status. 
M_ID :  ID 
Bit7 Bit6 Bit5 Bit4 Bit3 Bit2 Bit1 Bit0 
Change ID(1~253) 
Note : If Monitor ID reset bit of RS_Status is set, ignore M_ID 
  Depends on the product actual range can be differ 
  
● Ack 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack/Nak r-CMD Val 1 Val 2 
0xAA 0xFF 0x04 ‘A’ 0xFD RS_Status M_ID 
Check 
Sum 
RS_Status, M_ID : Same as above 
Note : Get cmd – In Ack, M_ID is current ID which is set. 
  
● Nak 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack/Nak r-CMD Val 1 Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xFF 0x03 ‘N’ 0xFD ERR 
ERR : Error Code which is displayed when error is 343ccurred. 
         Ex)  1. All ID Reset        : aa fd fe 02 10 00 
2. All Loopout disable  : aa fd fe 02 01 00 
3. Set ID #1           : aa fd 00 02 01 01 
4. Enable ID #1        : aa fd 01 02 00 01

Pattern Type

not a absolute simple color pattern type one can be controlled.

       During the pattern on/off or pattern changing, there transient video can be shown.

for set command and return as 0xff on Ack.

2.2 Internal Use Protocol 
2.2.01 Clock Control 
● Function 
Get/Set the device time. 
Note : It will be supported dependent on product specification.  
And there similar command 0xA7 Clock Control_MFM is exist 
  
● Get 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Check 
Sum 0xAA 0x01 0x00 
  
● Set 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Data 1 Data 2 Data 3 Data 4 
0xAA 0x01 0x06 Day Hour Time Minute 
Time Month 
Data 5 Data 6 Check 
Sum Year1 Year2 
  Day : Day value to be set on TV/Monitor ( 1 ~ 31 ) 
Month : Month value to be set on TV/Monitor ( 1 ~ 12 ) 
Year1 : Year value to be set on TV/Monitor (High Byte) 
Year2 : Year value to be set on TV/Monitor (Low Byte) 
Hour Time : Hour value to be set on TV/Monitor ( 1 ~ 12 ) 
Minute Time : Minute value to be set on TV/Monitor ( 0 ~ 59 ) 
  
● Ack 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack/Nak r-CMD Val 1 Val 2 
0xAA 0xFF 0x08 ‘A’ 0x01 Day Hour Time 
Val 3 Val 4 Val 5 Val 6 
Check 
Sum Minute 
Time Month Year1 Year2 
  Day, Month, Year1, Year2, Hour Time, Minute Time : Same as above 
Note : Hour, Minute Time if current time was not set on Monitor, 0xFF 
  
● Nak 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack/Nak r-CMD Val 1 Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xFF 0x03 ‘N’ 0x01 ERR 
  ERR : Error code that shows what occurred error is 
  
2.2.02 On Time Control 
● Function 
Get/Set the device on timer 
Note : It will be supported by product specification.  
And there similar commands are exist named as “Timerx Control_MFM” 
 
● Get 
 Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Check 
Sum 0xAA 0x02 0x00 
 
● Set 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Data 1 Data 2 Data 3 Data 4 
0xAA 0x02 0x06 0 N H Time N M Time N Time VR 
Data 5 Data 6 Check 
Sum N Time NF N Time SC 
  N H Time : On Time Hour value to be set on TV/Monitor ( 1 ~ 12 ) 
N M Time : On Time Minute value  to be set on TV/Monitor ( 0 ~ 59 ) 
N Time VR : Volume to be set on TV/Monitor. ( 0 ~ 100 ) 
N Time NF : On Time Activate/Inactivate value 
0x00 On Time Inactivate 0x01 On Time Activate 
N Time SC :  Source to be set on TV/Monitor (Refer  0x14 Input Source & App Control) 
  
● Ack 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack/Nak r-CMD Val 1 Val 2 
0xAA 0xFF 0x08 ‘A’ 0x02 0 N H Time 
Val 3 Val 4 Val 5 Val 6 Check 
Sum N M Time N Time VR N Time NF N Time SC 
  Val 1 ~ Val 6 : Same as above 
Note : N H Time Value, N M Time Value if current time was not set on Monitor, 0xFF 
  
● Nak 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack/Nak r-CMD Val 1 Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xFF 0x03 ‘N’ 0x02 ERR 
  ERR : Error code that shows what occurred error is

● Function 
Get the device info of panel, input source, videowall related things, rotation, screen size, model 
code, SW version, model name 
 
● Get 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Sub CMD Check 
Sum 0xAA 0x0A 0x01 0x81 
 
● Set 
Not Supported 
 
● Ack 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack r-CMD Sub CMD Val1 
0xAA 0xFF Variable ‘A’ 0x0A 0x81 Panel  On/Off 
Val2 Val3 Val4 Val5 Val6 Val7 Val8 Val9 
Source VideoWall 
On/Off 
VideoWall 
Position 
VideoWall 
Division 
VideoWall 
Mode Rotation ScreenSize Model 
Code 
Val10 Val11 Val12 Val13 … … … … 
SW Ver 
Length SW Ver1 … SW VerN 
Model 
Name 
Length 
Model 
Name 1 … Model 
Name N 
Check 
Sum 
Panel On/Off : Current panel status (0x01 : Off, 0x00 : On) 
Source : Current input source status(It is defined on input source command 0x14) 
VideoWall On/Off : Current status of videowall On/Off(0x01 : On, 0x00 : Off) 
VideoWall Position : Current serial no of videowall(Refer 0x89 Wall_Sno for detail) 
VideoWall Division : Current status videowall devision(Refer 0x89 Wall_Div for detail) 
VideoWall Mode : Current status of videowall mode(0x00 : Natural, 0x01 : Full) 
Rotation : Current status of source contents orientation mode 
(Refer 0xC8, Source Content Orientation Mode for detail) 
  ScreenSize : Screensize value of device(unit is inch) 
Model Code : Code of each mode(See 0x10 Model Number Control command for detail)  
  SW Ver Length : Length of followed SW ver data 
  SW Ver1 ~ SW VerN : SW version string, it includes project info and version info  
(Refer 0x0e for detail) 
  Model Name Length : Length of followed model name data 
  Model Name1 ~ Model NameN : Model name string(Refer 0x8e for detail)

Length 
CodeN Data 
Check Sum 
Code 
CODE DESCRIPTION 
0x00 Server URL : Server URL which has SW image 
Ex) http://10.88.43.36:8080/SWUTESTIMAGE/swuimage.bem 
0x01 SW Version : Model name and version info 
 Ex) T-KTM2LAKUC 0000.0 
0x02 File Size : Size of update image 
0x03 File Name : File name wants to update 
 Ex) swuimage.bem 
0x10 USB Main SW Update. There no following Data Length/Data in this option 
Code Data Length : Data length of Code Data 
Code Data : Code Data 
Note : In case of 0x10 USB Main SW Update, command should not have other code and data

ID 
Data Length Sub CMD

Sum 0xAA 0x1B 0x01 0x80 
 
● Set 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Sub CMD Data 1 Data 2 Data 3 
0xAA 0x1B Variable 0x80 Device1 ID Device1 IP 
1st Byte  
Device1 IP 
2nd Byte 
Data 4 Data 5 … … … … Data N 
Check  
Sum Device1 IP 
3rd Byte 
Device1 IP 
4th Byte …  DeviceN ID DeviceN IP (4 Bytes) 
Device ID 
0x00 - 0x01 Main Cabinet 1 
0x02 Main Cabinet 2 0x03 Main Cabinet 3 
0x04 Main Cabinet 4 0x05 Main Cabinet 5 
0x06 Main Cabinet 6 0x07 Main Cabinet 7 
0x08 Main Cabinet 8 0x09 Main Cabinet 9 
0x0A Main Cabinet 10 0x0B Main Cabinet 11 
0x0C Main Cabinet 12 0x0D Main Cabinet 13 
0x0E Main Cabinet 14 0x0F Main Cabinet 15 
0x10 Main Cabinet 16 0x11 - 
0xC0 - 0xC1 GroupA IG 
0xC2 GroupB IG 0xC3 GroupC IG 
0xC4 GroupD IG 0xC5 GroupE IG 
0xC6 GroupF IG 0xC7 GroupG IG 
0xC8 GroupH IG 0xC9 - 
NOTE :  
- Main Cabinet IP will be filled from cabinet CHA one. 
  Ex) On a certain product which support 4 cabinet ch, it needs to be map the main cabinet as 
          Ch A : Main Cabinet 1, Ch B : Main Cabinet 2, …, Ch D : Main Cabinet 4 
- Depends on the product spec there 1 or more main cabinet can be exist and in this case  
  lower ch cabinet should be mapped as lower main cabinet ID. 
Ex) On a TZ60 8K BOX product there 2 main cabinets are exist for 1 ch so those will be mapped 
    Ch A For : Main Cabinet 1, Ch A Back : Main Cabinet 2, …,  
Ch H For : Main Cabinet 15 and Ch H Back : Main Cabinet 16 
 
Device IP : IP address data. 
NOTE :  
- 1st byte of each data will be a MSB 
If IP address is 192.168.0.100 then 1st byte data will be a 0xc0 and 4th byte will be a 0x64 
- If all of the 4 bytes IP data are 0x00, that means invalid data

Note :  
. If there no code and data on the ACK packet, means related configuration is not set 
  . Optional means “Code Data Length” data can be exist or not by MSB of “Code” 
. Of the code field data, MSB 1bit is used for data length identification and rest 7bits are  
used for code. Pls don’t care the MSB bit on the table of “Code & Code Data” table 
. For the MSB bit pls refer bellowed description. 
 0 1 
1st MSB There no followed “Code Data Length” field 
and the data length will be 1. 
There followed “Code Data Length” field 
Example :  
. In case of “Cabinet ch / Box Pairing Configuration”, 
If code data is (1000 0001) then followed data will be like bellowed 
Data1 Data2 Data3 Data4 … … … … 
1000 0001 0xXX Module Power Test Result 
 
. In case of “Box Group Configuration”, related data format will be  
Data1 Data3 
0000 0000 SMPS Test 
Result 
 
 
Code & Code Data 
CODE DESCRIPTION 
0x00 
Box Group Configuration 
Bit7 Bit6 Bit5 Bit4 Bit3 Bit2 Bit1 Bit0 
Box Group ID 
Note : If Group ID is 0, then it means the box is not in any group 
0x01 
Cabinet Ch redundancy Configuration 
Bit7 Bit6 Bit5 Bit4 Bit3 Bit2 Bit1 Bit0 
0x00 : Forward 
0x01 : Reverse 
 
0x02 
1 Ch Redundancy (Get Only) 
Bit7 Bit6 Bit5 Bit4 Bit3 Bit2 Bit1 Bit0 
0x00 : Not Support 
0x01 : Support 
Note : If this data is not exist that means Not Support 
0x81 
Cabinet ch / Box Pairing Configuration 
Data Description 
1st Pairing Type 
0 : None 
1 : 2 Different Box Pairing 
2 : Hybrid Box Pairing 
2nd - If the pairing type is None there no following data 
Note : When the pairing mode is None following data will be “None” 
on get. 
- If pairing type is Hybrid Box Pairing then control the each cabinet ch 
screen position 
Data Description 
2nd Divided Screen Number, N 
3rd  Ch 0 position 
4th  Ch 1 position 
5th Ch 2 position 
… … 
Nth Ch N position 
Ch position Code(In case of Divided Screen Number is 4) 
Left Top : 
0 
Right Top : 
1 
Left Bottom : 
2 
Right Bottom : 
3 
Note : Ch position data 0xFF means not used. 
- If pairing type is 2 Different Box Pairing then control the info of 
paired device 
Data Description 
2nd Redundancy data count 
3rd  
Redundancy data(string) … 
Nth 
 
… 
Nth

… 
Sunrise / 
Sunset

Data N 
Sunrise / Sunset Location  : String data of location information . 
   The format of this string data is shown in the following form.  
   “Type1-Value1;Type2-Value2;…;TypeN-ValueN” 
   Each type and its values are passed on, and the distinction between types uses a  semicolon 
(‘;’). 
Examples : 
“Country- Korea, Republic of;Region -Gyeonggi;City -Suwon”  
“Latitude-37.29111;Longitude -127.00889”

2.2.21.30 Get Signal Info 
● Function 
Get the incoming signal info. 
 
● Get 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length  Sub CMD Check 
Sum 0xAA 0x21 0x01 0x30 
 
● Set  
Not Supported 
 
● Ack 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack r-CMD r-Sub CMD Data 1 
0xAA 0xFF Vairable 'A' 0x21 0x30 Code1 
Data 2 Data 3 … … … … … … 
Code1 
Data 
Length 
(Optional) 
Code1 Data … CodeN 
Code1 
Data 
Length 
(Optional) 
CodeN Data 
Check Sum 
Note :  
. If there no code and data on the ACK packet, means related feature is not supported. 
  . Optional means “Code Data Length” data can be exist or not by MSB of “Code” 
. Of the code field data, MSB is used for data length identification and rest 7bits are  
used for code. Pls don’t care the MSB bit on the table of “Code & Code Data” table 
. For the MSB bit pls refer bellowed description. 
 0 1 
1st MSB There no followed “Code Data Length” field 
and the data length will be 1. 
There will follow “Code Data Length” field 
Example :  
. In case of “H/V Resolution”, 
If code data is (1000 0000) then followed data will be like bellowed 
Data1 Data2 Data3 Data4 … … … … 
1000 0000  0xXX H/V Resolution 
 
. In case of “OSD On/Off”, related data format will be  
Data1 Data 2 
0000 0001  Scan Type 
 
 
Code & Code Data 
CODE DESCRIPTION 
0x00 - 
0x01 Scan Type  
0:interlace, 1:Progressive 
0x02 Horizontal Sync Polarity 
0 : Negative, 1 : Positive 
0x03 Vertical Sync Polarity 
0 : Negative, 1 : Positive 
0x04 
Color Format 
Code Description Code Description 
0x00 - 0x01 RGB444 
0x02 YUV444 0x03 YUV422 
0x04 YUV420 0x05 YC 
 
0x05 Sync Lock 
0 : Unlock, 1: Lock 
0x80 
H/V Resolution 
Data Description 
1st ~ 2nd Horizontal Resolution 
3rd ~ 4th Vertical Resolution 
 
0x81 
H/V Total 
Data Description 
1st ~ 2nd Horizontal Total 
3rd ~ 4th Vertical Total 
 
0x82 
H/V Frequency 
Data Description 
1st ~ 3rd Horizontal Frequency in Hz 
4th ~ 6th Vertical Frequency in Hz 
Note) This value express 100 times of actual value 
 
0x83 
H/V Start 
Data Description 
1st ~ 2nd Horizontal Start 
3rd ~ 4th Vertical Start 
 
 
● Nak 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length  Ack r-CMD r-Sub CMD Val1 
0xAA 0xFF 0x04 'N' 0x21 0x30 Err 
Check Sum 
Err : Error code that shows what occurred error is.

2.2.22.00 PC Screen Edge Detection 
● Function 
PC Screen edge detection event and its detail information handling 
 
● Get 
   Not Support 
 
● Set 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length  Sub CMD Data 1 Data 2 Data 3 
0xAA 0x22 Vairable 0x00 Type1 
Type1 Data 
Length 
(Optional) 
Type1 
Data 1st 
Val 2 … … … … … Val N 
Check 
Sum … Type1 Data 
Nth … Type N 
TypeN Data 
Length 
(Optional) 
TypeN Data 
Note :  
. Optional means “Data Length” data can be exist or not by MSB of “Code” 
. Of the code field data, MSB is used for data length identification and rest 6bits are  
used for type. Pls don’t care the MSB bit on the table of “Type & Type Data” table 
. For the MSB bit, pls refer bellowed description. 
 0 1 
1st MSB There no followed “Data Length” field and 
the data length will be 1Byte. 
There followed 1Byte “Data Length” field 
Example :  
. In case of none Data Length , 
Type Data1 
0xxx xxxx Data 
 
In case of data length 3bytes 
Tyoe Data Length Data1 Data2 Data3 
1xxx xxxx 0x03 Data 
 
 
Type & Type Data 
Type Data Description 
0x00 PC Screen ID - PC Screen ID which make edge detection event 
0x01 Horizontal Position – Mouse pointer horizontal position in % scale 
0x02 Vertical Position – Mouse pointer vertical position in % scale

Header Command 
ID 
Data Length  Ack r-CMD r-Sub CMD Val 1

(Optional)

ID 
Data Length Sub CMD Data1 Data2 Data3

Rotation 
Horizontal 
Pos High 
Data4 Data5 Data6 Data7 Data8 Data9 Data10 
Check 
Sum Horizontal 
Pos Low 
Vertical Pos 
High 
Vertical Pos 
Low Width High Width Low Height High Height Low 
Rotation : Same as defined info on 0xc8 sub command 0x81 Orientation Mode  
Videowall Rotation : It shows about rotation status of each devices of videowall. 
                 All reserved field should be 0. 
Bit8 Bit7 Bit6 Bit5 Bit4 Bit3 Bit2 Bit1 
Reserved Reserved Reserved Reserved 90 180 Portrait 
(270) 
Landscape 
(0) 
Note : Each bit will be 1, if threre exist at least 1 device which has related rotation 
    Ex) In the whole video wall, if there exist 180 rotation 2 devices and 270 rotation 1 device  
then this field will be 0x06. 
Horizontal Pos High/Low : Horizontal start postion of irregular videowall device 
Vertical Pos High/Low : Vertical start postion of irregular videowall device 
Width High/Low : Width of irregular videowall device 
Height High/Low : Height of irregular videowall device

2.2.C2 User Gamma Control 
● Function 
  On the ACM12 non applied model, set the device R/G/B Gamma Table 
Note : In case of ST Mars Platfor, R/G/B Gamma Tableis stored to E2PROM as 256WORDformat and 
it is interpolation as 1024WORD and used internally (because of E2PROM Size) 
  
● Set User Gamma 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Index Data 1 … Data 14 
0xAA 0xC2 0x0F Index       
Check Sum 
Index : Data 의 Gamma Group Index (1 group has 14 bytes length gamma data) 
Index 
(Decimal value) Group Number 
0 ~ 36 Red 0 ~ 36 
40 ~ 76 Green 0 ~ 36 
80 ~ 116 Blue 0 ~ 36 
Note : LFD can restore a Gamma table to E2PROM after get Index : 0xFF.

ACM12 : Use or not ACM12 (NUC, IDG, DICOM 등과 관련) 
0x00 Do not use ACM12, Do not support internal pattern  
0x01 Use ACM12, Support Internal Pattern 
0x02 Do not use ACM12, Support Internal Pattern 
0x03 Do not use ACM12, Support Internal Pattern with 
255 level 
Gamma Correction : Gamma correction is support or not on the non ACM12 applied model 
0x00 Do not use Gamma Correction 
0x01 Use Gamma Correction (UDA) 
0x02 Support MGA Gamma 
0x03 Support ACM Gamma 
Calibration Source : Calibration is supported by each source or not 
0x00 Do not support calibration by input video source 
0x01 Support calibration by input video source 
Calibration SpeedUp : Support or not a feature of calibration speed up 
0x00 Do not support a feature of calibration speed up 
0x01 Supports a feature of calibration speed up 
FW Update Protocol Version : FW update protocol type 
0x00 Do not Support FW Update protocol 
0x01 ~ 0xff Type of FW update protocol 
  Note : FW Update protocol has a unique protocol by each type. 
         Device support only 1 specific type of protocol. 
         If it returns data length as 7, that means FW update protocol dose not supported

used for code. Pls don’t care the MSB bit on the table of “Code & Code Data” table 
. For the MSB bit pls refer bellowed description. 
 0 1 
1st MSB There no followed “Code Data Length” field 
and the data length will be 1. 
There followed “Code Data Length” field 
Example :  
. In case of “Module Power Test Result”, 
If code data is (1000 0001) then followed data will be like bellowed 
Data1 Data2 Data3 Data4 … … … … 
1000 0001 0xXX Module Power Test Result 
 
. In case of “SMPS Test Result”, related data format will be  
Data1 Data3 
0000 0000 SMPS Test 
Result

2.2.D0.60 BroadCast Communication Device 
● Function 
Control the broadcast communication device range.  
When it is set, only the specified device need to reply for broadcast get communication.  
 
● Get 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Sub CMD Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xD0 0x01 0x60 
 
● Set  
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Sub CMD Data1 … Data32 
0xAA 0xD0 0x21 0x60 Device ID 1 … Device ID 32 
Check Sum 
Device ID : Each bit means about device MDC ID need to reply 
(Data assign from 32th data) 
Example) All attached device need to reply 
: All Device ID data(1st ~ 32th) will be 0xff 
Example) If device MDC id 2, 8, 34 need to reply 
: Device ID data 32th => 0x04, Device ID data 31th => 0x01, Device ID data 28th => 0x04 
 and all other data will be 0x00

Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack r-CMD Sub CMD Val 1

… Val 32 
Check Sum 
… Device ID 32

2.2.D0.8E Output Frame Rate Multiplication 
● Function 
Control the LED cabinet output frame rate, input video frame rate will be multipled and out by setting 
value 
 
● Get 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Sub CMD Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xD0 0x01 0x8E 
 
● Set 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Sub CMD Data1 
Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xD0 0x02 0x8E Frame Rate 
Multiple 
Frame Rate Multiple :  
0x00 x1 0x01 Up to MAX 
0x02 x2 0x03 x3 
0x04 x4 0x05 x5 
0x06 x6 0x07 x7 
0x08 x8 0x09 x9 
0x0A x10 0x0B x11 
0x0C x12 0x0D x13 
0x0E x14 0x0F x15 
0x10 x16 - - 
 Note : When default is set, output frame rate is automatically multipled up to max output frame rate 
of device. In case of incoming video frame rate and multiple optioin is over than device max output 
frame rate, device will update it as most high possible max frame rate related data internally 
Example) Incoming video frame rate is 60Hz and device max is 120Hz, when set it as x4 it will set to 
x4 but will be internally updated to possible max mode 2x. So it will be read as x2 on next read 
command 
 
● Ack 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack r-CMD Sub CMD Val 1 
0xAA 0xFF 0x04 'A' 0xD0 0x8E

Rate

2.2.D0.90 Factory WB (RGB) Control 
● Function 
  Control the cabinet white balance(RGB) 
 
● Get 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Sub CMD Data1 
Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xD0 0x02 0x90 Factory CC 
Position 
Factory CC Postion 
Bit7 Bit6 Bit5 Bit4 Bit3 Bit2 Bit1 Bit0 
X Y 
X : Red = 0, Green = 1, Blue = 2, All Y Line = 3 
Y : Red = 0, Green = 1, Blue = 2, All X Line = 3 
Note : Ex) If (X,Y) = 3,2 , Set/Get RB, GB, BB 
If (X,Y) = 1,3 , Set/Get GR, GG, GB 
If X/Y is 0x0F, current Cabinet CC value will be set as default on cabinet. 
Ex) Data1 is 0xff means cabinet CC will be set as default value.

2.2.D0.A6 Z-Card Attached Alived Cabinet Information 
● Function 
Get the zone card attached alived cabinet information 
 
● Get 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Sub CMD Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xD0 0x01 0xA6 
 
● Set 
   Not Supported 
 
● Ack 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack r-CMD Sub CMD Val  1 
0xAA 0xFF Variable 'A' 0xD0 0xA6 
Support 
Pilllar 
Count 
Val 2 … Val N Check 
Sum Aliving cabinet info 
Support Pilllar Count : Support pillar count by zone card 
Aliving cabinet info : String data of attached alived device info 
   - ; is a pillar separator 
   - each pillar data is exist as start ID, :, end ID. If there no device is alived there will no pillar data 
For example, if there 16 cabinets are exist on each pillar  
and the 4th pillar has no connected device, And if the alived device is like below for each  
  Forward : P0-8, P1-16, P2-10, P3-0, P4-0 
Reverse : P0-8, P1-0,  P2-6,  P3-0, P4-16 
Then each forward zone card and reverse zone card will return as 
=> Forward  2:9;2:17;2:11;;; 
   Reverse  10:17;;12:17;;2:17; 
   Note : This command is handled by zone card. So the command needs to be sent to zone card ID.

Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack r-CMD Sub CMD Val 1 
0xAA 0xFF 0x04 'N' 0xD0 0xA6 Err

Err : Error code that shows what occurred error is. 
  
2.2.D0.A8 Output Frame Rate Multiplication – Advanced (Shutter Sync) 
● Function 
Control the LED cabinet output frame rate with minute ratio, input video frame rate will be multipled 
and out by setting value 
 
● Get 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Sub CMD Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xD0 0x01 0xA8 
 
● Set 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Sub CMD Data 1 Data 2 
Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xD0 0x03 0xA8 Frame Rate Multiple 
Value 
Frame Rate Multiple Value : Value that controls the output frequency by multiplying the input 
frequency 
 Note :  
. The setting value is 1000 times the actual setting content. 
E.g.) When the setting value comes to 16667, it means 16.667 times operation.  
. It operates at the maximum output frequency supported by the device regardless of the set value 
E.g.) If the maximum output frequency of the device is 400 Hz,  
it operates at 400 Hz even if it is set 7 times in the 60 Hz input state. 
 
● Ack 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack r-CMD Sub CMD Val 1 
0xAA 0xFF 0x05 'A' 0xD0 0xA8 
Frame 
Rate 
Multiple 
Value High 
Val 2 
Check Sum Frame Rate 
Multiple 
Value Low 
Frame Rate Multiple : Same as above

Note : PQ data is used for overall video quality control including brightness. Brightness have a tight

module count as a way of resolution managing.

Count

Vertical 
Count

Module Vertical Count : PQ data mode vertical info which is selected 
Note : If module horizontal count is 1 and module vertical count is 3  
It means PQ data of 1x3 mode is working

2.2.D0.B4 Device Gamma & Factory Data Copy 
● Function

● Get   
  Not Support 
  
● Set 
Header Command 
ID 
Length Sub CMD Data1 
Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xD0 0x02 0xB4 Target 
Devide ID  
Target Devide ID : The target device ID that needs to copy data from source device 
       Source device will be automatically decided as  
         . If the target device ID is odd value then source device ID is target ID+1 
. If the target device ID is even value then source device ID is target ID-1 
. If the target device ID is even value and that is the last ID then  
source device ID is target ID-1. 
Note : This function is managed by main device so ID should be main device one always in actual.

2.2.D0.C4 Data ImportRequest 
● Function 
Request about data import session setup 
 
● Get  
  Not Supported 
 
● Set  
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Sub CMD Data1 Data2 Data3 
0xAA 0xD0 Variable 0xC4 Data Type TCP Port Number 
Data4 Data5 Data6 Data7 Data8 … Data39 Data40 
Data Size ID Info 1st 
Byte … ID Info 32th 
Byte 
Version 
Info 
Length 
Data41 … … … … … DataN 
Check 
Sum VerSion Info CRC 
Length CRC Data 
Data Type : Defined on 1B.A4 Check Software Version data type 
   TCP Port Number: TCP port number to fransfer the data 
Data Size : Data size to transfer 
ID Info 1st ~ 32th Byte : Each bit means about device MDC ID need to data transfer 
(Bit assign from 32th data) 
Example 1) Data needs to transfer to all attached device  
: all ID Info 1st ~ 32th Byte datawill be 0xff 
Example 1) Data needs to transfer to device MDC id 2, 8, 34 
: ID Info 32th => 0x04, ID Info 31th => 0x01, ID Info 28th => 0x04  
and all other data will be 0x00 
Version Info Length : Length data of version information 
      If there is no available version info is exist, this length value will be 0. 
Version Info Data 1st ~ N th : Version information of sending data 
CRC Length : Following CRC data length 
Note : IF CRC length is 0, it means there no valid CRC data 
CRC Data : CRC data of the transferring file

2.2.D1 Large Size & Simple Reply Functions

2.2.D2 Large Size & General Reply Functions

Data Description 
1st Order of data chunk 
2nd Total data chunk count

5th 
16Bits size number of N 3D MSB15 bits data (MSB will be ignored) … 
M-1th 
Mth 
16Bits size number of N 3D LSB15 bits data (MSB will be ignored) … 
Nth 
. Each command will handle 16375 MSB data and LSB data as maximum 
. When receive the last ordered data, whole data will be applied 
Example) If the total data has 35937 number of data. 
 - Data needs to be transferred by 3times 
  - Each command 1st, 2nd and 3rd data will be 
   1st command, 1st byte : 1, 2nd byte : 3, 3rd byte : 16375 
2nd command, 1st byte : 2, 2nd byte : 3, 3rd byte : 16375 
3rd command, 1st byte : 3, 2nd byte : 3, 3rd byte : 3187 
- Each command rest data will be 
   1st command, 16375 2bytes MSB data and LSB data 
2nd command, 16375 2bytes MSB data and LSB data  
3rd command, 3187 2bytes MSB data and LSB data 
File Name Length : File name length which will be transferred 
File Name Data : File name which will be transferred 
File Data Length : File data length which will be transferred 
File Data : File data which will be transferred

     For example, “1x2” has a data of Module Type – Extention : 0b0001 and Module Type : 0b001 
0x00 2x3 0x01 2x4 
0x02 4x3 0x03 8x3 
0x04 1x3 0x05 8x6 
0x06 4x6 0x07 4x12 
0x08 2x2 0x09 1x2 
0x0A 3x7 0x0B 4x7 
0x0C 4x8 0x0D 1x9 
0x0E ~ Defined in D0.83 Product Informataion - Modules 
Note :  
1. All reserved data need to fill as 0. 
  2..(Till 18 year model) 
For example, if cabinet is located center of UHD(3840x2160)screen  
then its position will be Position X : 1920, Position Y:1080 
    3. (From the 19 year model) Position X,Y data will be made as each channel internal position  
      For example, regardless its channel, position x,y will be 0,0 for left, top positioned cabinet.  
4. Each channel position is fixed like belowed 
   * 4 Channel Support Device 
     
* 8 Channel Support Device 
   
 5. Module Type data from0x0E and uppers are same with the info which is defined on D0.83 
Product Informataion - Modules

(Optional) CodeN Data 
Note :  
. If there no code and data on the ACK packet, means related feature is not supported. 
  . Optional means “Code Data Length” data can be exist or not by MSB of “Code” 
. Of the code field data, MSB 2bits are used for data length identification and rest 14bits are  
used for code. Pls don’t care the first 2 MSB bits on the table of “Code & Code Data” table 
. For the first 2MSB bits pls refer bellowed description. 
 0 1 
1st MSB There no followed “Code Data Length” field 
and the data length will be 1. 
There followed “Code Data Length” field 
2nd MSB In cas of MSB is 1, 
Followed “Code Data Length” field will be 
1byte data 
In cas of MSB is 1, 
Followed “Code Data Length” field wil be 
2bytes data 
Example :  
. In case of “Module Information”, 
If code data is (1000 0000 0000 1110) then followed data will be like bellowed 
Data1 Data2 Data3 Data4 … … … … 
1000 0000 0000 1110 0xXX Module Information 
 
If code data is (1100 0000 0000 1110) then followed data will be like bellowed 
Data1 Data2 Data3 Data4 Data5 … … … 
1100 0000 0000 1110 0xXXXX Module Information 
 
. In case of “OSD On/Off”, related data format will be  
Data1 Data2 Data3 
0000 0000 0000 0000 OSD On/Off

0x0009 Dynamic Peaking : Detail information is defined on 0x21 subcommand 0x04

0x000B Block WB(RGB) On/Off : Detail information is defined on 0xD0 subcommand 0x9D 
0x000C Cabinet WB(RGB) On/Off : Detail information is defined on 0xD0 subcommand 0x9E

0x00 
 . Set Only 
. 12 bytes fixed length data. Each 2bytes offset data is signed short format

3rd ~ 4th R2 Gain Offset

7th ~ 8th G2 Gain Offset 
9th ~ 10th B1 Gain Offset 
11th ~ 12th B2 Gain Offset 
 
0x01 
. Set Only 
. 1 byte data 
Data Description 
1st 0 : Reset, 1 : Apply 
 
0x02 
. Get Only 
. Data length is variable. Each 2bytes cal data is unsigned short format 
Data Description 
1st ~ 2nd Low calibration data 1 
… … 
(N-1)th ~ Nth Low calibration data N

2.2.E1 Peripheral Chip Control  
● Funcion 
Read/Write data for peripheral chip 
 
● Get 
  Not Support 
 
● Set 
  [Type 1] 
Header Command 
ID 
DataLength CMD Addr/Data ... Addr/Data 
0xAA 0xE1 0x04~0x61 Data      
Check 
Sum 
CMD 
Bit7 Bit6 Bit5 Bit4 Bit3 Bit2 Bit1 Bit0 
R/W Select Chip Write Mode / Read Mode 
R/W 
0x00 Read 0x01 Write 
Select Chip 
0x00 
NUC E2PROM ( 2byte Address, 1byte Data ) 
Write support mode : W-mode 0, W-mode 1 
Read support mode : R-mode 0, R-mode 1 
0x01 
NUC FPGA  ( 2byte Address, 2byte Data ) 
Write support mode : W-mode 0, W-mode 1, W-mode 2 
Read support mode : R-mode 0, R-mode 1 
Write Mode 
Mode 0 
(Address + Data) X N 
(Addr Byte, Data Byte) x ((Data Length - 1) /  
(Addr Byte + Data Byte)) 
1byte Data : Max 32 
2byte Data : Max 16 
Mode 1 
Start Address + ( Data X N ) 
Adress is auto increment. 
Start addr byte + Data byte x  
((Data Length - 1 - Addr Byte) / Data Length)  
1byte Data : Max 64 
2byte Data : Max 32 
Mode 2 
Burst Data write to same Address 
Add "Start / Packet Counter" 1byte 
Address in First Packet 
  
[Type 2] 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length CMD Start / 
Counter Addr /Data Addr /Data 
0xAA 0xE1 0x05~0x42 0x92 Data     
Check 
Sum 
Start / Counter 
Bit7 Bit6 Bit5 Bit4 Bit3 Bit2 Bit1 Bit0 
Start bit Remaining packet counter 
Start bit 
0x00 None start packet 0x01 Start packet : Add 2byte 
Addr 
Remaining packet counter 
- Left packet counter 
- Max 126 
- Last Packet value is 0 
- ex) start 0x8, end 0x0 if 9 packet. 
- this mode receive ACK only "enable start bit" or "remaining packet counter is 0" 
- NAK 
Err code 1 : resend all 
Err code 2 : resend marked packet 
Read Mode 
Mode 0 
send "Address X N", receive Ack "Data X N" 
1byte data : max 32 
2byte data : max 32 
Mode 1 
Request "start address" and N counter 
Receive Ack "Data X N" 
Adress is auto increment. 
1byte data : Max 64 
2byte data : Max 32

2.2.E2 Advanced IDG control 
● Function 
  Set the data for IDG control 
 
● Get 
  Not Support 
 
● Set 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Data 1 Data 2 Data 3 ...... 
0xAA 0xE2 0x10~0x81 CMD       
Data N Check 
Sum   
CMD :  
Bit7 Bit6 Bit5 Bit4 Bit3 Bit2 Bit1 Bit0 
Color Sampling Number Page Number Resered 
Color : Color type 
0x00 Red 
0x01 Green 
0x02 Blue 
Sampling Number : Number of Sample(1 Sampling Data = 2 bytes) 
0x00  8 Sample (16 bytes) 
0x01 16 Sample (32 bytes) 
0x02 32 Sample (64 bytes) 
0x03  64 Sample (128 bytes) 
0x04 128 Sample (256 bytes) 
0x05 256 Sample (512 bytes) 
Page Number : Page number(1 page can have 128 bytes.) 
0x00   1 ~ 128 byte 
0x01 129 ~ 256 byte 
0x02 257 ~ 384 byte 
0x03 385 ~ 512 byte

2.2.FE White Balance MDC Control 
● Function 
Control the white balance of the device. 
 
● Working Condition 
- Depends on each model spec it will be supported or not 
 
● Sub Command Table 
Sub CMD Function Sub CMD Function 
0x40 Request Custom Pattern Control 0x41 Custom Pattern Display by Name 
- - 0x51 Pattern Display 
0x52 Pattern Display with minute color level 0x53 Pattern Display by specific IP 
- - 0x61 WB Type(Get Only) 
0x62 White Balance Mode 0x63 20 Point Mode 
0x64 20 Point Interval - - 
- - 0x71 Make Default Color(Set Only) 
0x80 20 Point R/G/B Data 0x81 Red Gain 
- - 0x91 Green Gain 
- - 0xA1 Blue Gain 
- - 0xB1 Red Offset 
- - 0xC1 Green Offset 
- - 0xD1 Blue Offset 
- - 0xE1 Sub Brightness 
0xF2 White Balance Factory reset(Set Only) 0xF3 Reset 
Note : Grey colored commands are described in common section 
 
Note : There specific working mode for white balance control, that is

Annex A. Model dependency 
A.1 PIC_MODE definition 
● A model which is support **** Text , **** Video/Image and Calibration as picture mode on the menu 
1. If the picture mode on the menu is calibration, it will be treat as PIC_MODE_CALIB 
In case of picture mode in the menu is not calibration 
2. If current source is AV, TV or Component  
then the picture mode is treat as PIC_MODE_VIDEO regardless picture mode on the menu 
3. If current source is PC  
then the picture mode is treat as PIC_MODE_PC regardless picture mode on the menu 
   4. if current source is others(not listed in 2 or 3) 
then it will be treat as PIC_MODE_VIDEO when the picture mode in the menu is *** Video/Image 
or treat as PIC_MODE_PC when the picture mode in the menu is *** Text. 
  
A.2 H-Position Control 
● Function 
Personal Computer adjusts Horizontal Position of Device. 
 
● Working Condition 
- PC(D-Sub), BNC Only 
- When Video Wall is on or Zoom (0x39) is set, you can not control 
- HKIA support option is on 
 
● Get H-Position Status 
  Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Check 
Sum 0xAA 0x31 0x00 
 
● Set H-Position 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Data 1 Check 
Sum 0xAA 0x31 0x01 H-Pos 
H-Pos : Value of 0 ~ 100 
0 leftside max position 
1 ~ 49 percentage position between leftside max ~ default 
50 default position 
51 ~ 99 percentage position between default  ~ rightnside max  
100 rightnside max position 
  
● Ack 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack/Nak r-CMD Val 1 Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xFF 0x03 'A' 0x31 H-Pos 
H-Pos : Same as above 
  
● Nak 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack/Nak r-CMD Val 1 Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xFF 0x03 'N' 0x31 ERR 
ERR : Error code that shows what occurred error is 
  
A.3 V-Position Control 
● Function 
Personal Computer adjusts Vertical Position of TV/Monitor. 
  
● Working Condition 
- PC(D-Sub), BNC Only 
- When Video Wall is on or Zoom (0x39) is set, you can not control 
- HKIA support option is on 
 
● Get V-Position Status 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Check 
Sum 0xAA 0x32 0x00 
  
● Set V-Position 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Data 1 Check 
Sum 0xAA 0x32 0x01 V-Pos 
V-Pos : Value of 0 ~ 100 
0 upside max position 
1 ~ 49 percentage position between upside max ~ default 
50 default position 
51 ~ 99 percentage position between default ~ downside max 
100 downside max position 
 
● Ack 
Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack/Nak r-CMD Val 1 Check 
Sum 0xAA 0xFF 0x03 'A' 0x32 V-Pos 
V-Pos : Same as above

Header Command 
ID 
Data Length Ack/Nak r-CMD Val 1 Check
